# Requirements Document for 'WeatherForecast' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'WeatherForecast' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to view current weather conditions, check weekly forecasts, search for locations, receive weather alerts, and monitor air quality. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'WeatherForecast' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'WeatherForecast' web application will consist of the following eight pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Weather Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying current weather, quick location access, and navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: current-weather-summary** - Type: Div - Display of current weather conditions for default location.
  - **ID: search-location-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to location search page.
  - **ID: view-forecast-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to weekly forecast page.
  - **ID: view-alerts-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to weather alerts page.

### 2. Current Weather Page
- **Page Title**: Current Weather
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed current weather conditions for selected location.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: current-weather-page** - Type: Div - Container for the current weather page.
  - **ID: location-name** - Type: H1 - Display location name.
  - **ID: temperature-display** - Type: Div - Display current temperature.
  - **ID: weather-condition** - Type: Div - Display weather condition (sunny, rainy, cloudy, etc.).
  - **ID: humidity-info** - Type: Div - Display humidity percentage.
  - **ID: wind-speed-info** - Type: Div - Display wind speed.

### 3. Weekly Forecast Page
- **Page Title**: Weekly Forecast
- **Overview**: A page displaying weather forecast for the next 7 days.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: forecast-page** - Type: Div - Container for the forecast page.
  - **ID: forecast-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying daily forecasts with date, high temp, low temp, and condition.
  - **ID: location-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter forecast by location.
  - **ID: forecast-list** - Type: Div - Grid displaying forecast cards for each day.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 4. Location Search Page
- **Page Title**: Search Locations
- **Overview**: A page for users to search and select different locations.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.
  - **ID: location-search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search locations by city name or coordinates.
  - **ID: search-results** - Type: Div - List of search results displaying matching locations.
  - **ID: select-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to select a location (each result has this).
  - **ID: saved-locations-list** - Type: Div - Display of previously saved locations.

### 5. Weather Alerts Page
- **Page Title**: Weather Alerts
- **Overview**: A page displaying active weather alerts and warnings for selected locations.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: alerts-page** - Type: Div - Container for the alerts page.
  - **ID: alerts-list** - Type: Div - List of all active weather alerts with severity, description, and location.
  - **ID: severity-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter alerts by severity (All, Critical, High, Medium, Low).
  - **ID: location-filter-alerts** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter alerts by location.
  - **ID: acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}** - Type: Button - Button to acknowledge an alert (each alert has this).

### 6. Air Quality Page
- **Page Title**: Air Quality Index
- **Overview**: A page displaying air quality information and pollution levels for locations.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: air-quality-page** - Type: Div - Container for the air quality page.
  - **ID: aqi-display** - Type: Div - Display air quality index value (0-500).
  - **ID: aqi-description** - Type: Div - Display air quality description (Good, Moderate, Unhealthy, etc.).
  - **ID: pollution-details** - Type: Table - Table showing PM2.5, PM10, NO2, and other pollutants.
  - **ID: location-aqi-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by location.
  - **ID: health-recommendation** - Type: Div - Display health recommendations based on air quality.

### 7. Saved Locations Page
- **Page Title**: Saved Locations
- **Overview**: A page displaying all saved locations with quick weather access.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: saved-locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the saved locations page.
  - **ID: locations-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying saved locations with current temp and weather condition.
  - **ID: view-location-weather-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view weather for a location (each location has this).
  - **ID: remove-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove saved location (each location has this).
  - **ID: add-new-location-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new location.

### 8. Settings Page
- **Page Title**: Settings
- **Overview**: A page for users to configure temperature units, notification preferences, and default location.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: settings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the settings page.
  - **ID: temperature-unit-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select temperature unit (Celsius, Fahrenheit, Kelvin).
  - **ID: default-location-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to set default location.
  - **ID: alert-notifications-toggle** - Type: Checkbox - Toggle to enable/disable alert notifications.
  - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save settings changes.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'WeatherForecast' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Current Weather Data
- **File Name**: `current_weather.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  location_id|location_name|temperature|condition|humidity|wind_speed|last_updated
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30
  2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30
  3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30
  ```

### 2. Forecasts Data
- **File Name**: `forecasts.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  forecast_id|location_id|date|high_temp|low_temp|condition|precipitation|humidity
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60
  2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70
  3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85
  ```

### 3. Locations Data
- **File Name**: `locations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  location_id|location_name|latitude|longitude|country|timezone
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST
  2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT
  3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST
  ```

### 4. Weather Alerts Data
- **File Name**: `alerts.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  alert_id|location_id|alert_type|severity|description|start_time|end_time|is_acknowledged
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0
  2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0
  3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1
  ```

### 5. Air Quality Data
- **File Name**: `air_quality.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  aqi_id|location_id|aqi_index|pm25|pm10|no2|o3|last_updated
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30
  2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30
  3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30
  ```

### 6. Saved Locations Data
- **File Name**: `saved_locations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  saved_id|user_id|location_id|location_name|is_default
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|1|New York|1
  2|1|2|London|0
  3|2|3|Tokyo|1
  ```

# WeatherForecast Application Design Specification

## Section 1: Backend Routes Specification

### Route 1: `/`
- Method: GET
- Function Name: `redirect_to_dashboard`
- Description: Redirects from root URL to the dashboard page.
- Response: HTTP redirect to `/dashboard`

### Route 2: `/dashboard`
- Method: GET
- Function Name: `dashboard`
- Template: `dashboard.html`
- Description: Main dashboard page showing saved locations with current weather and alerts.
- Context Variables:
  - `saved_locations` (List[Dict]): List of saved location dicts.
    - Fields:
      - `location_id` (int)
      - `location_name` (str)
      - `latitude` (float)
      - `longitude` (float)
      - `country` (str)
      - `timezone` (str)
  - `current_weather` (List[Dict]): List of current weather per location.
    - Fields:
      - `location_id` (int)
      - `temperature` (int, Fahrenheit)
      - `condition` (str)
      - `humidity` (int, %)
      - `wind_speed` (int, mph)
      - `last_updated` (str, date YYYY-MM-DD)
  - `alerts` (List[Dict]): List of active alerts
    - Fields:
      - `alert_id` (int)
      - `location_id` (int)
      - `alert_type` (str)
      - `severity` (str)
      - `description` (str)
      - `start_time` (str, datetime)
      - `end_time` (str, datetime)
      - `is_acknowledged` (bool)

### Route 3: `/weather/current/<int:location_id>`
- Method: GET
- Function Name: `view_location_weather`
- Template: `current_weather.html`
- Description: Display detailed current weather for the specified location.
- Path Parameter:
  - `location_id` (int): The ID of the location.
- Context Variables:
  - `location` (Dict): Location details with fields as above.
  - `current_weather` (Dict): Current weather for the location.
  - `air_quality` (Dict): Air quality data for the location.
  - `alerts` (List[Dict]): Alerts filtered for the location.

### Route 4: `/weather/forecast/<int:location_id>`
- Method: GET
- Function Name: `view_forecast`
- Template: `forecast.html`
- Description: Show weather forecast for location.
- Parameters:
  - `location_id` (int)
- Context Variables:
  - `location` (Dict)
  - `forecasts` (List[Dict]) with fields:
    - `forecast_id` (int)
    - `location_id` (int)
    - `date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)
    - `high_temp` (int)
    - `low_temp` (int)
    - `condition` (str)
    - `precipitation` (int, %)
    - `humidity` (int, %)

### Route 5: `/air_quality/<int:location_id>`
- Method: GET
- Function Name: `view_air_quality`
- Template: `air_quality.html`
- Description: Show air quality for the location.
- Parameters:
  - `location_id` (int)
- Context Variables:
  - `location` (Dict)
  - `air_quality_details` (Dict) with fields:
    - `aqi_id` (int)
    - `location_id` (int)
    - `aqi_index` (int)
    - `pm25` (float)
    - `pm10` (float)
    - `no2` (float)
    - `o3` (float)
    - `last_updated` (str)

### Route 6: `/alerts`
- Method: GET
- Function Name: `alerts_page`
- Template: `alerts.html`
- Description: List all active alerts.
- Context Variables:
  - `alerts` (List[Dict]) with fields as in Route 2.

### Route 7: `/saved_locations`
- Method: GET
- Function Name: `saved_locations_page`
- Template: `saved_locations.html`
- Description: Manage saved locations.
- Context Variables:
  - `saved_locations` (List[Dict]) as Route 2.

### Route 8: `/settings`
- Method: GET, POST
- Function Name: `settings_page`
- Template: `settings.html`
- Description: User settings page to select temperature units and notification preferences.
- Context Variables:
  - `user_settings` (Dict) with keys:
    - `temperature_unit` (str): 'Celsius' or 'Fahrenheit'
    - `alert_notifications` (bool)

### Route 9: `/search`
- Method: GET
- Function Name: `search_locations`
- Template: `search.html`
- Description: Search for locations to add.
- Context Variables:
  - `search_results` (List[Dict]) with fields:
    - `location_id` (int)
    - `location_name` (str)
    - `latitude` (float)
    - `longitude` (float)
    - `country` (str)
    - `timezone` (str)


## Section 2: Frontend Templates Detail

### Template: `dashboard.html`
- Purpose: Show saved locations with current weather and alerts overview.
- Elements:
  - `saved-locations-list` (Div): Container listing saved locations.
  - Each location entry includes buttons:
    - `select-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): Chooses location for detailed view.
    - `remove-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): Removes location from saved.
  - `add-new-location-button` (Button): Navigate to location search page.
  - `location-filter-alerts` (Div): Filter controls for alerts.
  - `alerts-list` (Div): Listing active alerts.

- Navigation:
  - Add new location button -> `url_for('search_locations')`
  - Select location button navigates to detailed weather: `url_for('view_location_weather', location_id=location_id)`

- Context Variables:
  - `saved_locations`, `current_weather`, `alerts` as described.

- Dynamic content:
  - Loop over saved locations and alerts to render lists dynamically.
  - Conditional rendering if no saved locations or no alerts.

---

### Template: `current_weather.html`
- Purpose: Detailed current weather for a chosen location.
- Elements:
  - `current-weather-summary` (Div): Shows temperature, weather condition, humidity, wind speed.
  - `view-forecast-button` (Button): Navigates to forecast for the location.
  - `view-air-quality-button` (Button): Navigates to air quality page.
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Returns to dashboard.

- Navigation:
  - View forecast button -> `url_for('view_forecast', location_id=location_id)`
  - View air quality button -> `url_for('view_air_quality', location_id=location_id)`
  - Back to dashboard button -> `url_for('dashboard')`

- Context Variables:
  - `location`, `current_weather`, `air_quality`, `alerts`

- Dynamic content:
  - Display current weather data fields.

---

### Template: `forecast.html`
- Purpose: Show daily and weekly weather forecasts.
- Elements:
  - `forecast-table` (Table): Rows for each day with high/low temp, conditions, precipitation, humidity.
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigate back.

- Navigation:
  - Back to dashboard button -> `url_for('dashboard')`

- Context Variables:
  - `location`, `forecasts`

- Dynamic content:
  - Loop over `forecasts` to generate table rows.

---

  - `pollution-details` (Div): Detailed pollutant levels.
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)

- Navigation:
  - Back to dashboard button -> `url_for('dashboard')`

- Context Variables:
  - `location`, `air_quality_details`

- Dynamic content:
  - Display pollutant values dynamically.

- Elements:
  - `alerts-list` (Div/Table): List of alerts.
  - `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}` (Button) per alert: acknowledges alert.
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)

- Navigation:
  - Back to dashboard button -> `url_for('dashboard')`

- Context Variables:
  - `alerts`

- Dynamic content:
  - Loop over alerts.

  - `set-default-location-button-{location_id}` (Button) to mark default.
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)

## Section 3: Data Files Specification

### 1. `locations.txt`
- Pipe-delimited header:
  - `location_id|location_name|latitude|longitude|country|timezone`
- Each field:
  - `location_id` (int): Unique numeric ID.
  - `location_name` (str): City or area name.
  - `latitude` (float): Geographic coordinate.
  - `longitude` (float): Geographic coordinate.
  - `country` (str): Country name.
  - `timezone` (str): Timezone abbreviation.

- Example data:
```
3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST
2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT
1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST
```

### 2. `current_weather.txt`
- Header:
  - `location_id|temperature|condition|humidity|wind_speed|last_updated`
- Each field:
  - `location_id` (int)
  - `temperature` (int, Fahrenheit)
  - `condition` (str)
  - `humidity` (int, %)
  - `wind_speed` (int, mph)
  - `last_updated` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)

- Example data:
```
1|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20
3|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20
2|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20
```

### 3. `forecasts.txt`
- Header:
  - `forecast_id|location_id|date|high_temp|low_temp|condition|precipitation|humidity`
- Fields:
  - `forecast_id` (int)
  - `location_id` (int)
  - `date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)
  - `high_temp` (int)
  - `low_temp` (int)
  - `condition` (str)
  - `precipitation` (int, %)
  - `humidity` (int, %)

- Example data:
```
1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60
2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70
3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85
```

### 4. `air_quality.txt`
- Header:
  - `aqi_id|location_id|aqi_index|pm25|pm10|no2|o3|last_updated`
- Fields:
  - `aqi_id` (int)
  - `location_id` (int)
  - `aqi_index` (int)
  - `pm25` (float)
  - `pm10` (float)
  - `no2` (float)
  - `o3` (float)
  - `last_updated` (str)

- Example data:
```
2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20
3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20
1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20
```

### 5. `alerts.txt`
- Header:
  - `alert_id|location_id|alert_type|severity|description|start_time|end_time|is_acknowledged`
- Fields:
  - `alert_id` (int)
  - `location_id` (int)
  - `alert_type` (str)
  - `severity` (str): e.g. Low, Medium, High, Critical
  - `description` (str)
  - `start_time` (str, datetime format)
  - `end_time` (str, datetime format)
  - `is_acknowledged` (int, 0 or 1)

- Example data:
```
1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe weather|2025-01-20T14:30:00|2025-01-20T20:00:00|0
2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog|2025-01-21T06:00:00|2025-01-21T12:00:00|1
3|3|Wind|Medium|Strong wind gusts|2025-01-20T15:00:00|2025-01-20T21:00:00|0
```

### 6. `saved_locations.txt`
- Header:
  - `saved_id|user_id|location_id|location_name|is_default`
- Fields:
  - `saved_id` (int)
  - `user_id` (int)
  - `location_id` (int)
  - `location_name` (str)
  - `is_default` (int, 0 or 1)

- Example data:
```
1|1|1|New York|1
2|1|2|London|0
3|2|3|Tokyo|1
```

### 7. `user_settings.txt`
- Header:
  - `user_id|temperature_unit|alert_notifications`
- Fields:
  - `user_id` (int)
  - `temperature_unit` (str): 'Celsius' or 'Fahrenheit'
  - `alert_notifications` (int, 0 or 1)

- Example data:
```
1|Fahrenheit|1
2|Celsius|0
```

  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'WeatherForecast' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'WeatherForecast' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to view current weather conditions, check weekly forecasts, search for locations, receive weather alerts, and monitor air quality. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'WeatherForecast' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'WeatherForecast' web application will consist of the following eight pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Weather Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying current weather, quick location access, and navigation to all functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: current-weather-summary** - Type: Div - Display of current weather conditions for default location.   - **ID: search-location-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to location search page.   - **ID: view-forecast-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to weekly forecast page.   - **ID: view-alerts-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to weather alerts page.  ### 2. Current Weather Page - **Page Title**: Current Weather - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed current weather conditions for selected location. - **Elements**:   - **ID: current-weather-page** - Type: Div - Container for the current weather page.   - **ID: location-name** - Type: H1 - Display location name.   - **ID: temperature-display** - Type: Div - Display current temperature.   - **ID: weather-condition** - Type: Div - Display weather condition (sunny, rainy, cloudy, etc.).   - **ID: humidity-info** - Type: Div - Display humidity percentage.   - **ID: wind-speed-info** - Type: Div - Display wind speed.  ### 3. Weekly Forecast Page - **Page Title**: Weekly Forecast - **Overview**: A page displaying weather forecast for the next 7 days. - **Elements**:   - **ID: forecast-page** - Type: Div - Container for the forecast page.   - **ID: forecast-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying daily forecasts with date, high temp, low temp, and condition.   - **ID: location-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter forecast by location.   - **ID: forecast-list** - Type: Div - Grid displaying forecast cards for each day.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 4. Location Search Page - **Page Title**: Search Locations - **Overview**: A page for users to search and select different locations. - **Elements**:   - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.   - **ID: location-search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search locations by city name or coordinates.   - **ID: search-results** - Type: Div - List of search results displaying matching locations.   - **ID: select-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to select a location (each result has this).   - **ID: saved-locations-list** - Type: Div - Display of previously saved locations.  ### 5. Weather Alerts Page - **Page Title**: Weather Alerts - **Overview**: A page displaying active weather alerts and warnings for selected locations. - **Elements**:   - **ID: alerts-page** - Type: Div - Container for the alerts page.   - **ID: alerts-list** - Type: Div - List of all active weather alerts with severity, description, and location.   - **ID: severity-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter alerts by severity (All, Critical, High, Medium, Low).   - **ID: location-filter-alerts** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter alerts by location.   - **ID: acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}** - Type: Button - Button to acknowledge an alert (each alert has this).  ### 6. Air Quality Page - **Page Title**: Air Quality Index - **Overview**: A page displaying air quality information and pollution levels for locations. - **Elements**:   - **ID: air-quality-page** - Type: Div - Container for the air quality page.   - **ID: aqi-display** - Type: Div - Display air quality index value (0-500).   - **ID: aqi-description** - Type: Div - Display air quality description (Good, Moderate, Unhealthy, etc.).   - **ID: pollution-details** - Type: Table - Table showing PM2.5, PM10, NO2, and other pollutants.   - **ID: location-aqi-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by location.   - **ID: health-recommendation** - Type: Div - Display health recommendations based on air quality.  ### 7. Saved Locations Page - **Page Title**: Saved Locations - **Overview**: A page displaying all saved locations with quick weather access. - **Elements**:   - **ID: saved-locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the saved locations page.   - **ID: locations-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying saved locations with current temp and weather condition.   - **ID: view-location-weather-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view weather for a location (each location has this).   - **ID: remove-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove saved location (each location has this).   - **ID: add-new-location-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new location.  ### 8. Settings Page - **Page Title**: Settings - **Overview**: A page for users to configure temperature units, notification preferences, and default location. - **Elements**:   - **ID: settings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the settings page.   - **ID: temperature-unit-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select temperature unit (Celsius, Fahrenheit, Kelvin).   - **ID: default-location-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to set default location.   - **ID: alert-notifications-toggle** - Type: Checkbox - Toggle to enable/disable alert notifications.   - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save settings changes.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'WeatherForecast' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Current Weather Data - **File Name**: `current_weather.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   location_id|location_name|temperature|condition|humidity|wind_speed|last_updated   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30   2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30   3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30   ```  ### 2. Forecasts Data - **File Name**: `forecasts.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   forecast_id|location_id|date|high_temp|low_temp|condition|precipitation|humidity   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60   2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70   3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85   ```  ### 3. Locations Data - **File Name**: `locations.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   location_id|location_name|latitude|longitude|country|timezone   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST   2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT   3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST   ```  ### 4. Weather Alerts Data - **File Name**: `alerts.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   alert_id|location_id|alert_type|severity|description|start_time|end_time|is_acknowledged   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0   2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0   3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1   ```  ### 5. Air Quality Data - **File Name**: `air_quality.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   aqi_id|location_id|aqi_index|pm25|pm10|no2|o3|last_updated   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30   2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30   3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30   ```  ### 6. Saved Locations Data - **File Name**: `saved_locations.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   saved_id|user_id|location_id|location_name|is_default   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1|New York|1   2|1|2|London|0   3|2|3|Tokyo|1   ```
  [design_spec.md] # WeatherForecast Application Design Specification  ## Section 1: Backend Routes Specification  ### Route 1: `/` - Method: GET - Function Name: `redirect_to_dashboard` - Description: Redirects from root URL to the dashboard page. - Response: HTTP redirect to `/dashboard`  ### Route 2: `/dashboard` - Method: GET - Function Name: `dashboard` - Template: `dashboard.html` - Description: Main dashboard page showing saved locations with current weather and alerts. - Context Variables:   - `saved_locations` (List[Dict]): List of saved location dicts.     - Fields:       - `location_id` (int)       - `location_name` (str)       - `latitude` (float)       - `longitude` (float)       - `country` (str)       - `timezone` (str)   - `current_weather` (List[Dict]): List of current weather per location.     - Fields:       - `location_id` (int)       - `temperature` (int, Fahrenheit)       - `condition` (str)       - `humidity` (int, %)       - `wind_speed` (int, mph)       - `last_updated` (str, date YYYY-MM-DD)   - `alerts` (List[Dict]): List of active alerts     - Fields:       - `alert_id` (int)       - `location_id` (int)       - `alert_type` (str)       - `severity` (str)       - `description` (str)       - `start_time` (str, datetime)       - `end_time` (str, datetime)       - `is_acknowledged` (bool)  ### Route 3: `/weather/current/<int:location_id>` - Method: GET - Function Name: `view_location_weather` - Template: `current_weather.html` - Description: Display detailed current weather for the specified location. - Path Parameter:   - `location_id` (int): The ID of the location. - Context Variables:   - `location` (Dict): Location details with fields as above.   - `current_weather` (Dict): Current weather for the location.   - `air_quality` (Dict): Air quality data for the location.   - `alerts` (List[Dict]): Alerts filtered for the location.  ### Route 4: `/weather/forecast/<int:location_id>` - Method: GET - Function Name: `view_forecast` - Template: `forecast.html` - Description: Show weather forecast for location. - Parameters:   - `location_id` (int) - Context Variables:   - `location` (Dict)   - `forecasts` (List[Dict]) with fields:     - `forecast_id` (int)     - `location_id` (int)     - `date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)     - `high_temp` (int)     - `low_temp` (int)     - `condition` (str)     - `precipitation` (int, %)     - `humidity` (int, %)  ### Route 5: `/air_quality/<int:location_id>` - Method: GET - Function Name: `view_air_quality` - Template: `air_quality.html` - Description: Show air quality for the location. - Parameters:   - `location_id` (int) - Context Variables:   - `location` (Dict)   - `air_quality_details` (Dict) with fields:     - `aqi_id` (int)     - `location_id` (int)     - `aqi_index` (int)     - `pm25` (float)     - `pm10` (float)     - `no2` (float)     - `o3` (float)     - `last_updated` (str)  ### Route 6: `/alerts` - Method: GET - Function Name: `alerts_page` - Template: `alerts.html` - Description: List all active alerts. - Context Variables:   - `alerts` (List[Dict]) with fields as in Route 2.  ### Route 7: `/saved_locations` - Method: GET - Function Name: `saved_locations_page` - Template: `saved_locations.html` - Description: Manage saved locations. - Context Variables:   - `saved_locations` (List[Dict]) as Route 2.  ### Route 8: `/settings` - Method: GET, POST - Function Name: `settings_page` - Template: `settings.html` - Description: User settings page to select temperature units and notification preferences. - Context Variables:   - `user_settings` (Dict) with keys:     - `temperature_unit` (str): 'Celsius' or 'Fahrenheit'     - `alert_notifications` (bool)  ### Route 9: `/search` - Method: GET - Function Name: `search_locations` - Template: `search.html` - Description: Search for locations to add. - Context Variables:   - `search_results` (List[Dict]) with fields:     - `location_id` (int)     - `location_name` (str)     - `latitude` (float)     - `longitude` (float)     - `country` (str)     - `timezone` (str)   ## Section 2: Frontend Templates Detail  ### Template: `dashboard.html` - Purpose: Show saved locations with current weather and alerts overview. - Elements:   - `saved-locations-list` (Div): Container listing saved locations.   - Each location entry includes buttons:     - `select-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): Chooses location for detailed view.     - `remove-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): Removes location from saved.   - `add-new-location-button` (Button): Navigate to location search page.   - `location-filter-alerts` (Div): Filter controls for alerts.   - `alerts-list` (Div): Listing active alerts.  - Navigation:   - Add new location button -> `url_for('search_locations')`   - Select location button navigates to detailed weather: `url_for('view_location_weather', location_id=location_id)`  - Context Variables:   - `saved_locations`, `current_weather`, `alerts` as described.  - Dynamic content:   - Loop over saved locations and alerts to render lists dynamically.   - Conditional rendering if no saved locations or no alerts.  ---  ### Template: `current_weather.html` - Dynamic content:   - Display current weather data fields.  ---  ### Template: `forecast.html` - Purpose: Show daily and weekly weather forecasts. - Elements:   - `forecast-table` (Table): Rows for each day with high/low temp, conditions, precipitation, humidity.   - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Navigate back.  - Navigation:   - Back to dashboard button -> `url_for('dashboard')`  - Context Variables:   - `location`, `forecasts`  - Dynamic content:   - Loop over `forecasts` to generate table rows.  ---  ### Template: `air_quality.html` - Navigation:   - Back to dashboard button -> `url_for('dashboard')`  - Context Variables:   - `alerts`  - Dynamic content:   - Loop over alerts.  ---  ### Template: `saved_locations.html` - Purpose: Manage saved locations. - Elements:   - `saved-locations-list` (Div): Shows saved locations.   - `remove-location-button-{location_id}` (Button) to remove.   - `set-default-location-button-{location_id}` (Button) to mark default.   - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)  - Navigation:   - Back to dashboard button -> `url_for('dashboard')`  - Context Variables:   - `saved_locations`  - Dynamic content:   - Loop saved locations.  ---  ### Template: `settings.html` - Purpose: User preferences form. - Elements:   - `temperature-unit-select` (Dropdown): Celsius, Fahrenheit.   - `alert-notifications-toggle` (Checkbox): On/Off.   - `save-settings-button` (Button): Save changes.   - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)  - Navigation:   - Back to dashboard button -> `url_for('dashboard')`  - Context Variables:   - `user_settings`  - Dynamic content:   - Set form defaults from `user_settings`.  ---  ### Template: `search.html` - `wind_speed` (int, mph)   - `last_updated` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)  - Example data: ``` 1|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 3|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 2|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 ```  ### 3. `forecasts.txt` - Header:   - `forecast_id|location_id|date|high_temp|low_temp|condition|precipitation|humidity` - Fields:   - `forecast_id` (int)   - `location_id` (int)   - `date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)   - `high_temp` (int)   - `low_temp` (int)   - `condition` (str)   - `precipitation` (int, %)   - `humidity` (int, %)  - Example data: ``` 1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60 2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70 3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85 ```  ### 4. `air_quality.txt` - Header:   - `aqi_id|location_id|aqi_index|pm25|pm10|no2|o3|last_updated` - Fields:   - `aqi_id` (int)   - `location_id` (int)   - `aqi_index` (int)   - `pm25` (float)   - `pm10` (float)   - `no2` (float)   - `o3` (float)   - `last_updated` (str)  - Example data: ``` 2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 ```  ### 5. `alerts.txt` - Header:   - `alert_id|location_id|alert_type|severity|description|start_time|end_time|is_acknowledged` - Fields:   - `alert_id` (int)   - `location_id` (int)   - `alert_type` (str)   - `severity` (str): e.g. Low, Medium, High, Critical   - `description` (str)   - `start_time` (str, datetime format)   - `end_time` (str, datetime format)   - `is_acknowledged` (int, 0 or 1)  - Example data: ``` 1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe weather|2025-01-20T14:30:00|2025-01-20T20:00:00|0 2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog|2025-01-21T06:00:00|2025-01-21T12:00:00|1 3|3|Wind|Medium|Strong wind gusts|2025-01-20T15:00:00|2025-01-20T21:00:00|0 ```  ### 6. `saved_locations.txt` - Header:   - `saved_id|user_id|location_id|location_name|is_default` - Fields:   - `saved_id` (int)   - `user_id` (int)   - `location_id` (int)   - `location_name` (str)   - `is_default` (int, 0 or 1)  - Example data: ``` 1|1|1|New York|1 2|1|2|London|0 3|2|3|Tokyo|1 ```  ### 7. `user_settings.txt` - Header:   - `user_id|temperature_unit|alert_notifications` - Fields:   - `user_id` (int)   - `temperature_unit` (str): 'Celsius' or 'Fahrenheit'   - `alert_notifications` (int, 0 or 1)  - Example data: ``` 1|Fahrenheit|1 2|Celsius|0 ```  ---  This completes the detailed specification for backend routes including URLs, HTTP methods, function names, templates and context variables; frontend templates with all required element IDs and descriptions; and all data files with exact field order, types, and sample data.

# Requirements Document for 'WeatherForecast' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'WeatherForecast' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to view current weather conditions, check weekly forecasts, search for locations, receive weather alerts, and monitor air quality. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'WeatherForecast' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'WeatherForecast' web application will consist of the following eight pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Weather Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying current weather, quick location access, and navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: current-weather-summary** - Type: Div - Display of current weather conditions for default location.
  - **ID: search-location-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to location search page.
  - **ID: view-forecast-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to weekly forecast page.
  - **ID: view-alerts-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to weather alerts page.

### 2. Current Weather Page
- **Page Title**: Current Weather
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed current weather conditions for selected location.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: current-weather-page** - Type: Div - Container for the current weather page.
  - **ID: location-name** - Type: H1 - Display location name.
  - **ID: temperature-display** - Type: Div - Display current temperature.
  - **ID: weather-condition** - Type: Div - Display weather condition (sunny, rainy, cloudy, etc.).
  - **ID: humidity-info** - Type: Div - Display humidity percentage.
  - **ID: wind-speed-info** - Type: Div - Display wind speed.

### 3. Weekly Forecast Page
- **Page Title**: Weekly Forecast
- **Overview**: A page displaying weather forecast for the next 7 days.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: forecast-page** - Type: Div - Container for the forecast page.
  - **ID: forecast-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying daily forecasts with date, high temp, low temp, and condition.
  - **ID: location-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter forecast by location.
  - **ID: forecast-list** - Type: Div - Grid displaying forecast cards for each day.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 4. Location Search Page
- **Page Title**: Search Locations
- **Overview**: A page for users to search and select different locations.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.
  - **ID: location-search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search locations by city name or coordinates.
  - **ID: search-results** - Type: Div - List of search results displaying matching locations.
  - **ID: select-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to select a location (each result has this).
  - **ID: saved-locations-list** - Type: Div - Display of previously saved locations.

### 5. Weather Alerts Page
- **Page Title**: Weather Alerts
- **Overview**: A page displaying active weather alerts and warnings for selected locations.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: alerts-page** - Type: Div - Container for the alerts page.
  - **ID: alerts-list** - Type: Div - List of all active weather alerts with severity, description, and location.
  - **ID: severity-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter alerts by severity (All, Critical, High, Medium, Low).
  - **ID: location-filter-alerts** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter alerts by location.
  - **ID: acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}** - Type: Button - Button to acknowledge an alert (each alert has this).

### 6. Air Quality Page
- **Page Title**: Air Quality Index
- **Overview**: A page displaying air quality information and pollution levels for locations.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: air-quality-page** - Type: Div - Container for the air quality page.
  - **ID: aqi-display** - Type: Div - Display air quality index value (0-500).
  - **ID: aqi-description** - Type: Div - Display air quality description (Good, Moderate, Unhealthy, etc.).
  - **ID: pollution-details** - Type: Table - Table showing PM2.5, PM10, NO2, and other pollutants.
  - **ID: location-aqi-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by location.
  - **ID: health-recommendation** - Type: Div - Display health recommendations based on air quality.

### 7. Saved Locations Page
- **Page Title**: Saved Locations
- **Overview**: A page displaying all saved locations with quick weather access.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: saved-locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the saved locations page.
  - **ID: locations-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying saved locations with current temp and weather condition.
  - **ID: view-location-weather-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view weather for a location (each location has this).
  - **ID: remove-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove saved location (each location has this).
  - **ID: add-new-location-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new location.

### 8. Settings Page
- **Page Title**: Settings
- **Overview**: A page for users to configure temperature units, notification preferences, and default location.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: settings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the settings page.
  - **ID: temperature-unit-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select temperature unit (Celsius, Fahrenheit, Kelvin).
  - **ID: default-location-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to set default location.
  - **ID: alert-notifications-toggle** - Type: Checkbox - Toggle to enable/disable alert notifications.
  - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save settings changes.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'WeatherForecast' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Current Weather Data
- **File Name**: `current_weather.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  location_id|location_name|temperature|condition|humidity|wind_speed|last_updated
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30
  2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30
  3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30
  ```

### 2. Forecasts Data
- **File Name**: `forecasts.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  forecast_id|location_id|date|high_temp|low_temp|condition|precipitation|humidity
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60
  2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70
  3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85
  ```

### 3. Locations Data
- **File Name**: `locations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  location_id|location_name|latitude|longitude|country|timezone
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST
  2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT
  3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST
  ```

### 4. Weather Alerts Data
- **File Name**: `alerts.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  alert_id|location_id|alert_type|severity|description|start_time|end_time|is_acknowledged
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0
  2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0
  3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1
  ```

### 5. Air Quality Data
- **File Name**: `air_quality.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  aqi_id|location_id|aqi_index|pm25|pm10|no2|o3|last_updated
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30
  2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30
  3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30
  ```

### 6. Saved Locations Data
- **File Name**: `saved_locations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  saved_id|user_id|location_id|location_name|is_default
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|1|New York|1
  2|1|2|London|0
  3|2|3|Tokyo|1
  ```

# WeatherForecast Application Design Specification

## Section 1: Backend Routes Specification

### Route 1: `/`
- Method: GET
- Function Name: `redirect_to_dashboard`
- Description: Redirects from root URL to the dashboard page.
- Response: HTTP redirect to `/dashboard`

### Route 2: `/dashboard`
- Method: GET
- Function Name: `dashboard`
- Template: `dashboard.html`
- Description: Main dashboard page showing saved locations with current weather and alerts.
- Context Variables:
  - `saved_locations` (List[Dict]): List of saved location dicts.
    - Fields:
      - `location_id` (int)
      - `location_name` (str)
      - `latitude` (float)
      - `longitude` (float)
      - `country` (str)
      - `timezone` (str)
  - `current_weather` (List[Dict]): List of current weather per location.
    - Fields:
      - `location_id` (int)
      - `temperature` (int, Fahrenheit)
      - `condition` (str)
      - `humidity` (int, %)
      - `wind_speed` (int, mph)
      - `last_updated` (str, date YYYY-MM-DD)
  - `alerts` (List[Dict]): List of active alerts
    - Fields:
      - `alert_id` (int)
      - `location_id` (int)
      - `alert_type` (str)
      - `severity` (str)
      - `description` (str)
      - `start_time` (str, datetime)
      - `end_time` (str, datetime)
      - `is_acknowledged` (bool)

### Route 3: `/weather/current/<int:location_id>`
- Method: GET
- Function Name: `view_location_weather`
- Template: `current_weather.html`
- Description: Display detailed current weather for the specified location.
- Path Parameter:
  - `location_id` (int): The ID of the location.
- Context Variables:
  - `location` (Dict): Location details with fields as above.
  - `current_weather` (Dict): Current weather for the location.
  - `air_quality` (Dict): Air quality data for the location.
  - `alerts` (List[Dict]): Alerts filtered for the location.

### Route 4: `/weather/forecast/<int:location_id>`
- Method: GET
- Function Name: `view_forecast`
- Template: `forecast.html`
- Description: Show weather forecast for location.
- Parameters:
  - `location_id` (int)
- Context Variables:
  - `location` (Dict)
  - `forecasts` (List[Dict]) with fields:
    - `forecast_id` (int)
    - `location_id` (int)
    - `date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)
    - `high_temp` (int)
    - `low_temp` (int)
    - `condition` (str)
    - `precipitation` (int, %)
    - `humidity` (int, %)

### Route 5: `/air_quality/<int:location_id>`
- Method: GET
- Function Name: `view_air_quality`
- Template: `air_quality.html`
- Description: Show air quality for the location.
- Parameters:
  - `location_id` (int)
- Context Variables:
  - `location` (Dict)
  - `air_quality_details` (Dict) with fields:
    - `aqi_id` (int)
    - `location_id` (int)
    - `aqi_index` (int)
    - `pm25` (float)
    - `pm10` (float)
    - `no2` (float)
    - `o3` (float)
    - `last_updated` (str)

### Route 6: `/alerts`
- Method: GET
- Function Name: `alerts_page`
- Template: `alerts.html`
- Description: List all active alerts.
- Context Variables:
  - `alerts` (List[Dict]) with fields as in Route 2.

### Route 7: `/saved_locations`
- Method: GET
- Function Name: `saved_locations_page`
- Template: `saved_locations.html`
- Description: Manage saved locations.
- Context Variables:
  - `saved_locations` (List[Dict]) as Route 2.

### Route 8: `/settings`
- Method: GET, POST
- Function Name: `settings_page`
- Template: `settings.html`
- Description: User settings page to select temperature units and notification preferences.
- Context Variables:
  - `user_settings` (Dict) with keys:
    - `temperature_unit` (str): 'Celsius' or 'Fahrenheit'
    - `alert_notifications` (bool)

### Route 9: `/search`
- Method: GET
- Function Name: `search_locations`
- Template: `search.html`
- Description: Search for locations to add.
- Context Variables:
  - `search_results` (List[Dict]) with fields:
    - `location_id` (int)
    - `location_name` (str)
    - `latitude` (float)
    - `longitude` (float)
    - `country` (str)
    - `timezone` (str)

## Section 3: Data Files Specification

### 1. `locations.txt`
- Pipe-delimited header:
  - `location_id|location_name|latitude|longitude|country|timezone`
- Each field:
  - `location_id` (int): Unique numeric ID.
  - `location_name` (str): City or area name.
  - `latitude` (float): Geographic coordinate.
  - `longitude` (float): Geographic coordinate.
  - `country` (str): Country name.
  - `timezone` (str): Timezone abbreviation.

- Example data:
```
3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST
2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT
1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST
```

### 2. `current_weather.txt`
- Header:
  - `location_id|temperature|condition|humidity|wind_speed|last_updated`
- Each field:
  - `location_id` (int)
  - `temperature` (int, Fahrenheit)
  - `condition` (str)
  - `humidity` (int, %)
  - `wind_speed` (int, mph)
  - `last_updated` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)

- Example data:
```
1|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20
3|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20
2|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20
```

### 3. `forecasts.txt`
- Header:
  - `forecast_id|location_id|date|high_temp|low_temp|condition|precipitation|humidity`
- Fields:
  - `forecast_id` (int)
  - `location_id` (int)
  - `date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)
  - `high_temp` (int)
  - `low_temp` (int)
  - `condition` (str)
  - `precipitation` (int, %)
  - `humidity` (int, %)

- Example data:
```
1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60
2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70
3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85
```

### 4. `air_quality.txt`
- Header:
  - `aqi_id|location_id|aqi_index|pm25|pm10|no2|o3|last_updated`
- Fields:
  - `aqi_id` (int)
  - `location_id` (int)
  - `aqi_index` (int)
  - `pm25` (float)
  - `pm10` (float)
  - `no2` (float)
  - `o3` (float)
  - `last_updated` (str)

- Example data:
```
2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20
3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20
1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20
```

### 5. `alerts.txt`
- Header:
  - `alert_id|location_id|alert_type|severity|description|start_time|end_time|is_acknowledged`
- Fields:
  - `alert_id` (int)
  - `location_id` (int)
  - `alert_type` (str)
  - `severity` (str): e.g. Low, Medium, High, Critical
  - `description` (str)
  - `start_time` (str, datetime format)
  - `end_time` (str, datetime format)
  - `is_acknowledged` (int, 0 or 1)

- Example data:
```
1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe weather|2025-01-20T14:30:00|2025-01-20T20:00:00|0
2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog|2025-01-21T06:00:00|2025-01-21T12:00:00|1
3|3|Wind|Medium|Strong wind gusts|2025-01-20T15:00:00|2025-01-20T21:00:00|0
```

### 6. `saved_locations.txt`
- Header:
  - `saved_id|user_id|location_id|location_name|is_default`
- Fields:
  - `saved_id` (int)
  - `user_id` (int)
  - `location_id` (int)
  - `location_name` (str)
  - `is_default` (int, 0 or 1)

- Example data:
```
1|1|1|New York|1
2|1|2|London|0
3|2|3|Tokyo|1
```

### 7. `user_settings.txt`
- Header:
  - `user_id|temperature_unit|alert_notifications`
- Fields:
  - `user_id` (int)
  - `temperature_unit` (str): 'Celsius' or 'Fahrenheit'
  - `alert_notifications` (int, 0 or 1)

- Example data:
```
1|Fahrenheit|1
2|Celsius|0

# Requirements Document for 'WeatherForecast' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'WeatherForecast' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to view current weather conditions, check weekly forecasts, search for locations, receive weather alerts, and monitor air quality. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'WeatherForecast' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'WeatherForecast' web application will consist of the following eight pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Weather Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying current weather, quick location access, and navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: current-weather-summary** - Type: Div - Display of current weather conditions for default location.
  - **ID: search-location-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to location search page.
  - **ID: view-forecast-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to weekly forecast page.
  - **ID: view-alerts-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to weather alerts page.

### 2. Current Weather Page
- **Page Title**: Current Weather
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed current weather conditions for selected location.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: current-weather-page** - Type: Div - Container for the current weather page.
  - **ID: location-name** - Type: H1 - Display location name.
  - **ID: temperature-display** - Type: Div - Display current temperature.
  - **ID: weather-condition** - Type: Div - Display weather condition (sunny, rainy, cloudy, etc.).
  - **ID: humidity-info** - Type: Div - Display humidity percentage.
  - **ID: wind-speed-info** - Type: Div - Display wind speed.

### 3. Weekly Forecast Page
- **Page Title**: Weekly Forecast
- **Overview**: A page displaying weather forecast for the next 7 days.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: forecast-page** - Type: Div - Container for the forecast page.
  - **ID: forecast-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying daily forecasts with date, high temp, low temp, and condition.
  - **ID: location-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter forecast by location.
  - **ID: forecast-list** - Type: Div - Grid displaying forecast cards for each day.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 4. Location Search Page
- **Page Title**: Search Locations
- **Overview**: A page for users to search and select different locations.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.
  - **ID: location-search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search locations by city name or coordinates.
  - **ID: search-results** - Type: Div - List of search results displaying matching locations.
  - **ID: select-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to select a location (each result has this).
  - **ID: saved-locations-list** - Type: Div - Display of previously saved locations.

### 5. Weather Alerts Page
- **Page Title**: Weather Alerts
- **Overview**: A page displaying active weather alerts and warnings for selected locations.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: alerts-page** - Type: Div - Container for the alerts page.
  - **ID: alerts-list** - Type: Div - List of all active weather alerts with severity, description, and location.
  - **ID: severity-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter alerts by severity (All, Critical, High, Medium, Low).
  - **ID: location-filter-alerts** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter alerts by location.
  - **ID: acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}** - Type: Button - Button to acknowledge an alert (each alert has this).

### 6. Air Quality Page
- **Page Title**: Air Quality Index
- **Overview**: A page displaying air quality information and pollution levels for locations.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: air-quality-page** - Type: Div - Container for the air quality page.
  - **ID: aqi-display** - Type: Div - Display air quality index value (0-500).
  - **ID: aqi-description** - Type: Div - Display air quality description (Good, Moderate, Unhealthy, etc.).
  - **ID: pollution-details** - Type: Table - Table showing PM2.5, PM10, NO2, and other pollutants.
  - **ID: location-aqi-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by location.
  - **ID: health-recommendation** - Type: Div - Display health recommendations based on air quality.

### 7. Saved Locations Page
- **Page Title**: Saved Locations
- **Overview**: A page displaying all saved locations with quick weather access.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: saved-locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the saved locations page.
  - **ID: locations-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying saved locations with current temp and weather condition.
  - **ID: view-location-weather-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view weather for a location (each location has this).
  - **ID: remove-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove saved location (each location has this).
  - **ID: add-new-location-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new location.

### 8. Settings Page
- **Page Title**: Settings
- **Overview**: A page for users to configure temperature units, notification preferences, and default location.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: settings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the settings page.
  - **ID: temperature-unit-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select temperature unit (Celsius, Fahrenheit, Kelvin).
  - **ID: default-location-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to set default location.
  - **ID: alert-notifications-toggle** - Type: Checkbox - Toggle to enable/disable alert notifications.
  - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save settings changes.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'WeatherForecast' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Current Weather Data
- **File Name**: `current_weather.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  location_id|location_name|temperature|condition|humidity|wind_speed|last_updated
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30
  2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30
  3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30
  ```

### 2. Forecasts Data
- **File Name**: `forecasts.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  forecast_id|location_id|date|high_temp|low_temp|condition|precipitation|humidity
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60
  2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70
  3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85
  ```

### 3. Locations Data
- **File Name**: `locations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  location_id|location_name|latitude|longitude|country|timezone
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST
  2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT
  3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST
  ```

### 4. Weather Alerts Data
- **File Name**: `alerts.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  alert_id|location_id|alert_type|severity|description|start_time|end_time|is_acknowledged
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0
  2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0
  3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1
  ```

### 5. Air Quality Data
- **File Name**: `air_quality.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  aqi_id|location_id|aqi_index|pm25|pm10|no2|o3|last_updated
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30
  2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30
  3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30
  ```

### 6. Saved Locations Data
- **File Name**: `saved_locations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  saved_id|user_id|location_id|location_name|is_default
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|1|New York|1
  2|1|2|London|0
  3|2|3|Tokyo|1
  ```

Route: `/settings` (User Settings)\n- Method: GET, POST\n- Template: `settings.html`\n- Purpose: User preferences such as unit selection (Celsius/Fahrenheit), notification toggles.\n- Context Data:\n  - `user_settings`: dictionary with preferences like `temperature_unit`, `alert_notifications`\n\n### 8. # Requirements Document for 'WeatherForecast' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'WeatherForecast' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to view current weather conditions, check weekly forecasts, search for locations, receive weather alerts, and monitor air quality. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'WeatherForecast' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'WeatherForecast' web application will consist of the following eight pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Weather Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying current weather, quick location access, and navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: current-weather-summary** - Type: Div - Display of current weather conditions for default location.
  - **ID: search-location-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to location search page.
  - **ID: view-forecast-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to weekly forecast page.
  - **ID: view-alerts-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to weather alerts page.

### 2. Current Weather Page
- **Page Title**: Current Weather
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed current weather conditions for selected location.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: current-weather-page** - Type: Div - Container for the current weather page.
  - **ID: location-name** - Type: H1 - Display location name.
  - **ID: temperature-display** - Type: Div - Display current temperature.
  - **ID: weather-condition** - Type: Div - Display weather condition (sunny, rainy, cloudy, etc.).
  - **ID: humidity-info** - Type: Div - Display humidity percentage.
  - **ID: wind-speed-info** - Type: Div - Display wind speed.

### 3. Weekly Forecast Page
- **Page Title**: Weekly Forecast
- **Overview**: A page displaying weather forecast for the next 7 days.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: forecast-page** - Type: Div - Container for the forecast page.
  - **ID: forecast-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying daily forecasts with date, high temp, low temp, and condition.
  - **ID: location-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter forecast by location.
  - **ID: forecast-list** - Type: Div - Grid displaying forecast cards for each day.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 4. Location Search Page
- **Page Title**: Search Locations
- **Overview**: A page for users to search and select different locations.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.
  - **ID: location-search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search locations by city name or coordinates.
  - **ID: search-results** - Type: Div - List of search results displaying matching locations.
  - **ID: select-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to select a location (each result has this).
  - **ID: saved-locations-list** - Type: Div - Display of previously saved locations.

### 5. Weather Alerts Page
- **Page Title**: Weather Alerts
- **Overview**: A page displaying active weather alerts and warnings for selected locations.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: alerts-page** - Type: Div - Container for the alerts page.
  - **ID: alerts-list** - Type: Div - List of all active weather alerts with severity, description, and location.
  - **ID: severity-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter alerts by severity (All, Critical, High, Medium, Low).
  - **ID: location-filter-alerts** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter alerts by location.
  - **ID: acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}** - Type: Button - Button to acknowledge an alert (each alert has this).

### 6. Air Quality Page
- **Page Title**: Air Quality Index
- **Overview**: A page displaying air quality information and pollution levels for locations.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: air-quality-page** - Type: Div - Container for the air quality page.
  - **ID: aqi-display** - Type: Div - Display air quality index value (0-500).
  - **ID: aqi-description** - Type: Div - Display air quality description (Good, Moderate, Unhealthy, etc.).
  - **ID: pollution-details** - Type: Table - Table showing PM2.5, PM10, NO2, and other pollutants.
  - **ID: location-aqi-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by location.
  - **ID: health-recommendation** - Type: Div - Display health recommendations based on air quality.

- **Overview**: A page displaying all saved locations with quick weather access.

  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'WeatherForecast' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Current Weather Data
- **File Name**: `current_weather.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  location_id|location_name|temperature|condition|humidity|wind_speed|last_updated
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30
  2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30
  3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30
  ```

### 2. Forecasts Data
- **File Name**: `forecasts.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  forecast_id|location_id|date|high_temp|low_temp|condition|precipitation|humidity
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60
  2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70
  3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85
  ```

### 3. Locations Data
- **File Name**: `locations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  location_id|location_name|latitude|longitude|country|timezone
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST
  2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT
  3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST
  ```

### 4. Weather Alerts Data
- **File Name**: `alerts.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  alert_id|location_id|alert_type|severity|description|start_time|end_time|is_acknowledged
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0
  2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0
  3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1
  ```

### 5. Air Quality Data
- **File Name**: `air_quality.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  aqi_id|location_id|aqi_index|pm25|pm10|no2|o3|last_updated
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30
  2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30
  3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30
  ```

### 6. Saved Locations Data
- **File Name**: `saved_locations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  saved_id|user_id|location_id|location_name|is_default
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|1|New York|1
  2|1|2|London|0
  3|2|3|Tokyo|1
  ```

  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'WeatherForecast' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'WeatherForecast' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to view current weather conditions, check weekly forecasts, search for locations, receive weather alerts, and monitor air quality. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'WeatherForecast' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'WeatherForecast' web application will consist of the following eight pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Weather Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying current weather, quick location access, and navigation to all functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: current-weather-summary** - Type: Div - Display of current weather conditions for default location.   - **ID: search-location-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to location search page.   - **ID: view-forecast-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to weekly forecast page.   - **ID: view-alerts-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to weather alerts page.  ### 2. Current Weather Page - **Page Title**: Current Weather - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed current weather conditions for selected location. - **Elements**:   - **ID: current-weather-page** - Type: Div - Container for the current weather page.   - **ID: location-name** - Type: H1 - Display location name.   - **ID: temperature-display** - Type: Div - Display current temperature.   - **ID: weather-condition** - Type: Div - Display weather condition (sunny, rainy, cloudy, etc.).   - **ID: humidity-info** - Type: Div - Display humidity percentage.   - **ID: wind-speed-info** - Type: Div - Display wind speed.  ### 3. Weekly Forecast Page - **Page Title**: Weekly Forecast - **Overview**: A page displaying weather forecast for the next 7 days. - **Elements**:   - **ID: forecast-page** - Type: Div - Container for the forecast page.   - **ID: forecast-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying daily forecasts with date, high temp, low temp, and condition.   - **ID: location-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter forecast by location.   - **ID: forecast-list** - Type: Div - Grid displaying forecast cards for each day.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 4. Location Search Page - **Page Title**: Search Locations - **Overview**: A page for users to search and select different locations. - **Elements**:   - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.   - **ID: location-search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search locations by city name or coordinates.   - **ID: search-results** - Type: Div - List of search results displaying matching locations.   - **ID: select-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to select a location (each result has this).   - **ID: saved-locations-list** - Type: Div - Display of previously saved locations.  ### 5. Weather Alerts Page - **Page Title**: Weather Alerts - **Overview**: A page displaying active weather alerts and warnings for selected locations. - **Elements**:   - **ID: alerts-page** - Type: Div - Container for the alerts page.   - **ID: alerts-list** - Type: Div - List of all active weather alerts with severity, description, and location.   - **ID: severity-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter alerts by severity (All, Critical, High, Medium, Low).   - **ID: location-filter-alerts** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter alerts by location.   - **ID: acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}** - Type: Button - Button to acknowledge an alert (each alert has this).  ### 6. Air Quality Page - **Page Title**: Air Quality Index - **Overview**: A page displaying air quality information and pollution levels for locations. - **Elements**:   - **ID: air-quality-page** - Type: Div - Container for the air quality page.   - **ID: aqi-display** - Type: Div - Display air quality index value (0-500).   - **ID: aqi-description** - Type: Div - Display air quality description (Good, Moderate, Unhealthy, etc.).   - **ID: pollution-details** - Type: Table - Table showing PM2.5, PM10, NO2, and other pollutants.   - **ID: location-aqi-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by location.   - **ID: health-recommendation** - Type: Div - Display health recommendations based on air quality.  ### 7. Saved Locations Page - **Page Title**: Saved Locations - **Overview**: A page displaying all saved locations with quick weather access. - **Elements**:   - **ID: saved-locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the saved locations page.   - **ID: locations-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying saved locations with current temp and weather condition.   - **ID: view-location-weather-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view weather for a location (each location has this).   - **ID: remove-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove saved location (each location has this).   - **ID: add-new-location-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new location.  ### 8. Settings Page - **Page Title**: Settings - **Overview**: A page for users to configure temperature units, notification preferences, and default location. - **Elements**:   - **ID: settings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the settings page.   - **ID: temperature-unit-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select temperature unit (Celsius, Fahrenheit, Kelvin).   - **ID: default-location-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to set default location.   - **ID: alert-notifications-toggle** - Type: Checkbox - Toggle to enable/disable alert notifications.   - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save settings changes.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'WeatherForecast' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Current Weather Data - **File Name**: `current_weather.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   location_id|location_name|temperature|condition|humidity|wind_speed|last_updated   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30   2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30   3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30   ```  ### 2. Forecasts Data - **File Name**: `forecasts.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   forecast_id|location_id|date|high_temp|low_temp|condition|precipitation|humidity   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60   2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70   3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85   ```  ### 3. Locations Data - **File Name**: `locations.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   location_id|location_name|latitude|longitude|country|timezone   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST   2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT   3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST   ```  ### 4. Weather Alerts Data - **File Name**: `alerts.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   alert_id|location_id|alert_type|severity|description|start_time|end_time|is_acknowledged   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0   2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0   3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1   ```  ### 5. Air Quality Data - **File Name**: `air_quality.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   aqi_id|location_id|aqi_index|pm25|pm10|no2|o3|last_updated   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30   2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30   3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30   ```  ### 6. Saved Locations Data - **File Name**: `saved_locations.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   saved_id|user_id|location_id|location_name|is_default   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1|New York|1   2|1|2|London|0   3|2|3|Tokyo|1   ```
